<review>I want to thank the Paso Robles Country Club for really going above and beyond for making my wedding day so special. To Amy (venue/wedding coordinator) she is absolutely amazing, a beautiful person inside and out who genuinely cares about your day. My uncle had passed away the day before my wedding, and I was blown away with the amount of love and support I was shown. I was so worried and stressed to tell them I wont be having my wedding. They weren't concerned one bit about me giving them the news, they weren't concerned about them losing out on an event they could have had. They were so understanding, and told me to reach out to them when I was ready to pick another date and if they had to move some things around, they would. I was blown away. Thank you so much to both Scott and Amy for being there every step of the way. I'm so grateful and so lucky to have had my wedding here. It was absolutely beautiful, communication was so easy, received so much help, so much advice. So much space for you and the girls to get ready. So chic so rustic, modern so perfect! Huge vanity, huge mirrors, fridge, counter space, couch, closet, room, restroom, 2 oversized sink vanity, pub table area. < review>
We went on a Saturday night about 6:30. They were very busy but we were seated in a few minutes.  Chips and salsa (very good) were quickly brought to our table. Service was rather slow but I guess that was because they were so busy. Once we ordered, the food was brought pretty quickly. I would rate the food as very good, the presentation as average, the price as reasonable . My biggest complaint would be the cleanliness. The tile floors were very dirty for a restaurant and the walls are in need of fresh paint. It makes you wonder about the cleanliness of the kitchen. We are visiting the area and it was our first time there.< /review>
